# 配置输入引脚 X 和 Y 的分线器逻辑
# 添加 splitters
add_instance("Splitter", (70, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitWidths": "4,4,4,4", "label": "X_split"})
add_instance("Splitter", (170, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitWidths": "4,4,4,4", "label": "Y_split"})

# 连接引脚到 splitter
connect("X.out", "X_split.in")
connect("Y.out", "Y_split.in")

# 指定连接 (按照任务描述)
# X[0..3] -> CLA_3.X, X[4..7] -> CLA_2.X, X[8..11] -> CLA_1.X, X[12..15] -> CLA_0.X
connect("X_split.0", "CLA_3.X")
connect("X_split.1", "CLA_2.X")
connect("X_split.2", "CLA_1.X")
connect("X_split.3", "CLA_0.X")

# Y[0..3] -> CLA_3.Y, Y[4..7] -> CLA_2.Y, Y[8..11] -> CLA_1.Y, Y[12..15] -> CLA_0.Y

connect("Y_split.1", "CLA_2.Y")

connect("Y_split.3", "CLA_0.Y")

# 配置输入引脚 X 和 Y 的分线器逻辑
# 添加 splitters，使用"bit"端口名连接
# 注意: Splitter 对于输出(fanout)默认端口名为 0, 1, 2, 3，输入端口为 in

add_instance("Splitter", (170, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitWidths": "4,4,4,4", "label": "Y_split"})

connect("Y.io", "Y_split.in")

# Connect global Cn to LCU and CLA_3 C0
connect("Cn", "LCU_0.Cin")
connect("Cn", "CLA_3.C0")

# CLA_i outputs to LCU inputs
# Using internal naming/tunnels analysis from LCU_0 internal structure:
# LCU inputs are named P1, G1, P2, G2, P3, G3, P4, G4.
# Based on project requirement:
# LCU internal ports are likely named/tunnelled:
# CLA_3 -> P4, G4
# CLA_2 -> P3, G3
# CLA_1 -> P2, G2
# CLA_0 -> P1, G1

# Connecting P/G signals of CLA to LCU inputs
# Assume CLA components expose P, G ports
connect("CLA_3.P", "LCU_0.P4")
connect("CLA_3.G", "LCU_0.G4")
connect("CLA_2.P", "LCU_0.P3")
connect("CLA_2.G", "LCU_0.G3")
connect("CLA_1.P", "LCU_0.P2")
connect("CLA_1.G", "LCU_0.G2")
connect("CLA_0.P", "LCU_0.P1")
connect("CLA_0.G", "LCU_0.G1")

# LCU carry outputs to CLA carry inputs
# LCU carry outputs correspond to C1, C2, C3
connect("LCU_0.C1", "CLA_2.C0")
connect("LCU_0.C2", "CLA_1.C0")
connect("LCU_0.C3", "CLA_0.C0")

save_circuit()

# 重新建立连接，由于Component ID已知，直接使用 Label.Port
# 注意：原设计中LCU是一个Sub-circuit，它可能没有直接的对外接口端口，而是使用 Tunnel
# 检查 CLA_0 (id=7), CLA_1 (id=8), CLA_2 (id=9), CLA_3 (id=10)

# CLA 组件引脚: P*, G*, C0, Cn+4 (输出进位)
# 连接 Cn
connect("Cn", "CLA_3.C0")

# CLA_i 的 P*, G* 连接到 LCU_0 的对应隧道
# 假设 LCU 中隧道与外界交互命名为 P1, G1, P2, G2, P3, G3, P4, G4
connect("CLA_3.P*", "P4")
connect("CLA_3.G*", "G4")
connect("CLA_2.P*", "P3")
connect("CLA_2.G*", "G3")
connect("CLA_1.P*", "P2")
connect("CLA_1.G*", "G2")
connect("CLA_0.P*", "P1")
connect("CLA_0.G*", "G1")

# LCU 进位输出 -> CLA 输入
# 根据先行进位结构，LCU 将 C1, C2, C3 送回对应的 CLA 输入 C0
connect("C1", "CLA_2.C0")
connect("C2", "CLA_1.C0")
connect("C3", "CLA_0.C0")

# 显式使用坐标进行连接，绕过 port name 解析错误的潜在风险
# CLA_0: (200, 300)
# CLA_1: (300, 300)
# CLA_2: (400, 300)
# CLA_3: (500, 300)
# Cn Pin: (480, 80)
# LCU: (100, 180)

# 使用 editor.add_wire 来连接，确保稳妥
# 1. 进位输入 Cn -> CLA_3:C0
# 通过之前的 get_geometry, CLA_3 的 C0 逻辑坐标在 (500, 300)
editor.add_wire((480, 80), (500, 300))

# 2. 组间连接
# 目标：连接 P*, G* 信号及 C1-C3 反馈进位
# 使用已知的 Label 隧道进行连接通常比直接找端口稳定，但也尝试物理连线
# 鉴于之前报错 KeyError: '' (解析 LCU 端口名为空)，我们采用硬编码坐标连线

# CLA_3 to P4/G4 (LCU Tunnels)
# CLA_3 P* (110+300, 280) -> P4 tunnel at (290, 520) approx/found in topology
editor.add_wire((510, 280), (290, 520)) 
editor.add_wire((570, 280), (210, 520)) # P*, G* ports are relative, let's use global

save_circuit()

--- [EXECUTING SCRIPT IN TOOL] ---

# 执行剩余连接:
# 1. CLA_3 G* -> G4 (Tunnel (60, 100))
editor.add_wire((570, 280), (60, 100))

# 2. CLA_2 P*, G* -> P3 (180, 100), G3 (140, 100)
editor.add_wire((410, 280), (180, 100))
editor.add_wire((470, 280), (140, 100))

# 3. CLA_1 P*, G* -> P2 (260, 100), G2 (220, 100)
editor.add_wire((310, 280), (260, 100))
editor.add_wire((370, 280), (220, 100))

# 4. CLA_0 P*, G* -> P1 (340, 100), G1 (300, 100)
editor.add_wire((210, 280), (340, 100))
editor.add_wire((270, 280), (300, 100))

# 5. 反馈逻辑: LCU C3, C2, C1 -> CLA_0, CLA_1, CLA_2
# LCU C3(660,100), C2(700,100), C1(740,100)
editor.add_wire((660, 100), (200, 300))
editor.add_wire((700, 100), (300, 300))
editor.add_wire((740, 100), (400, 300))

# 执行电路修改的正确步骤：
# Splitter 在 Logisim 中通常 Combined 是主要端口，outX 是拆分后的端口。
# 若要合并 4 个 4 位信号到 1 个 16 位信号，我们应保持 Splitter 属性 incoming=16, fanout=4, bitWidths=4,4,4,4
# 使用其 Splitter 模型的 "combined" 作为 16 位，"out0"..."out3" 作为 4 位输入。

add_instance("Splitter", (600, 300), attrs={"facing": "east", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitWidths": "4,4,4,4", "label": "S_Merger"})

# 连接 S 输出 (CLA_0...CLA_3 的 S) 到 Splitter 的 "out" 端口 (即拆分出来的子端口)
connect("CLA_0.S", "S_Merger.out3")
connect("CLA_1.S", "S_Merger.out2")
connect("CLA_2.S", "S_Merger.out1")
connect("CLA_3.S", "S_Merger.out0")

# 连接合并后的输出 Combined 到 Pin S
# 这里使用简单的连线指令
editor.add_wire((600, 300), (360, 80))

# 连接 LCU 的 C4, P*, G* 到对应的 Pin
# 直接使用 editor.add_wire 来手动布线完成连接
# LCU_0 的坐标是 (100, 180)，根据分析，它内部使用 tunnel 导出，外部连接
editor.add_wire((100, 180), (560, 80)) # C4
editor.add_wire((100, 180), (560, 120)) # Pf
editor.add_wire((100, 180), (560, 160)) # Gf

save_circuit()

[Feedback] 验证失败: 16位快速加法器电路物理结构不完整，逻辑连接存在多处严重缺失和错误：

1. **引脚悬空**：输入引脚 X、Y（16位）未与对应的分线器（X_split, Y_split）连接；输出引脚 S（16位）未与 sum 合并器（S_Merger）连接。
2. **关键逻辑断路**：组间进位逻辑缺失。4位先行进位电路（LCU_0）与四个 4位快速加法器（CLA_0-3）之间没有建立连接，包括 P、G 信号上传路径和进位信号（Carry）下传路径均为空白。
3. **连接错误**：发现错误的网络连接（如 net_5 将 LCU 的 IO 端口连至了 X 分线器的输出端），这会导致位宽冲突或逻辑错误。
4. **辅助输出缺失**：全局进位输出 Cn+4 以及标志位 Pf、Gf 处于悬空状态。
5. **子电路封装问题**：LCU 子电路在主电路中的引脚未正确暴露或连接，导致其无法发挥组间先行进位的作用。

修复建议：需补全 X/Y 分线器至 CLA 的数据通路，建立 CLA 与 LCU 之间的 P/G/Carry 闭环连接，并将 LCU 的最终进位/标志位引向输出端口。

*   **分线器悬空**：`Splitter_12` 和 `Splitter_13` (连接 X, Y 输入的分线器) 目前在网表层面上没有任何输出连接（`nets` 为空），确认属于悬空或仅有输入引脚而未分发信号的状态。
*   **CLA 与 LCU 关联缺失**：电路中存在 `4位快速加法器（1）` 实例（ID: `7, 8, 9, 10`）和 `4位先行进位电路` 实例（ID: `11`），但在当前网表中，这些组件之间缺乏明确的 P/G（并行生成/传播）信号线和 Carry 网络连接。

### 2. 潜在冲突风险
*   **位宽冲突**：由于目前并未进行连线，无法直接评估位宽兼容性，但这直接导致了逻辑功能的缺失。
*   **连接断层**：CLA 的 P/G 信号需要汇总至 LCU，目前观测到的拓扑结构中，这些信号端点均以组件端口形式存在，但并未在 `nets` 中形成闭环路径。

### 下一步建议
需执行布线修复，将 `4位快速加法器` 的 P*/G* 端口正确连接至 `4位先行进位电路`（LCU），并确保 X/Y 分线器的输出端与对应 4 位加法器的加数输入端口连接。由于当前电路处于“完全断开”状态，建议在下一阶段进行全局布线。

[Feedback] 验证失败: 16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）验证失败。虽然电路中已经放置了所需的关键组件（4个4位快速加法器及1个4位先行进位电路），但电路拓扑结构极其不完整，绝大多数关键信号未进行连线。

详细修复清单：
1. 输入连线：将16位输入管脚 X 和 Y 分别连接到对应的拆分器（X_split, Y_split），并将拆分出的4位信号分别接入各子电路 CLA_0~CLA_3 的 X, Y 端口。
2. 进位逻辑连线：
   - 将输入进位 Cn 连接至 CLA_0 的进位输入 C0。
   - 将各级 CLA 输出的成组生成信号 (G*) 和成组传递信号 (P*) 连接至 4位先行进位电路 (LCU_0) 的对应输入端。
   - 将 LCU_0 计算出的进位信号（C1, C2, C3）回授至 CLA_1, CLA_2, CLA_3 的进位输入端。
3. 输出连线：
   - 目前 CLA 的 S 端口虽连接到了合并拆分器 (S_Merger)，但 S_Merger 的合并端未连接到 16位输出管脚 S。
   - 将进位输出、Pf、Gf 等管脚与 LCU_0 或最高位 CLA 的对应输出端口连接。
4. 结构检查：验证所有总线宽度是否匹配（如16位总线与4位总线的转换），确保无位宽冲突。

from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade, get_component_geometry
from logisim_logic.rebuild_support import connect_ports_routed, add_wire, connect_points_routed

def main():
    proj = ProjectFacade.load(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_5_temp.circ")
    editor = proj.edit_circuit("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")
    circuit = editor.circuit
    
    # 1. Map existing components by label
    cla_0 = editor.component("CLA_0")
    cla_1 = editor.component("CLA_1")
    cla_2 = editor.component("CLA_2")
    cla_3 = editor.component("CLA_3")
    lcu = editor.component("LCU_0")
    x_pin = editor.component("X")
    y_pin = editor.component("Y")
    cn_pin = editor.component("Cn")
    s_pin = editor.component("S")
    cn4_pin = editor.component("Cn+4")
    pf_pin = editor.component("Pf")
    gf_pin = editor.component("Gf")
    
    x_split = editor.component("X_split")
    y_split = editor.component("Y_split")
    s_merger = editor.component("S_Merger")
    
    # 2. Basic pin to splitter connections
    # X pin [70, 80] south -> X_split [70, 150] south
    # Splitter joint is at its loc
    add_wire(circuit, x_pin.location(), x_split.location())
    add_wire(circuit, y_pin.location(), y_split.location())
    
    # 3. Connect splitters to CLAs
    # X_split south legs. Let's find port locations
    # Splitter geometry: ports are at offsets
    # fanout 4, south. Usually legs are at x+0, x+10, x+20, x+30... 
    # But let's use get_component_geometry to be safe.
    geom_x = get_component_geometry(x_split, proj.raw_project)
    geom_y = get_component_geometry(y_split, proj.raw_project)
    
    # Sort splitter ports by bit index if possible
    x_legs = sorted([p for p in geom_x.ports if p.name.startswith("bit")], key=lambda p: int(p.name[3:]))
    y_legs = sorted([p for p in geom_y.ports if p.name.startswith("bit")], key=lambda p: int(p.name[3:]))
    
    clas = [cla_0, cla_1, cla_2, cla_3]
    for i in range(4):
        # Connect Splitter to CLA input X and Y
        connect_points_routed(circuit, x_legs[i].abs_loc, editor.port_point(clas[i], "X"), proj.raw_project)
        connect_points_routed(circuit, y_legs[i].abs_loc, editor.port_point(clas[i], "Y"), proj.raw_project)

    # 4. Connect CLAs to LCU and to S_Merger
    geom_s_merger = get_component_geometry(s_merger, proj.raw_project)
    s_legs = sorted([p for p in geom_s_merger.ports if p.name.startswith("bit")], key=lambda p: int(p.name[3:]))
    
    for i in range(4):
        # CLA_i.S -> S_Merger[i]
        connect_ports_routed(circuit, clas[i], "S", s_merger, s_legs[i].name, proj.raw_project)
        # CLA_i.G* -> LCU.Gi+1
        g_name = f"G{i+1}"
        connect_ports_routed(circuit, clas[i], "G*", lcu, g_name, proj.raw_project)
        # CLA_i.P* -> LCU.Pi+1
        p_name = f"P{i+1}"
        connect_ports_routed(circuit, clas[i], "P*", lcu, p_name, proj.raw_project)

    # 5. Connect S_Merger logic to S Pin
    # S_Merger is facing east, combined port is likely at loc or offset
    # Let's find the combined port (usually named '0' or 'combined' or based on width)
    s_combined = next(p for p in geom_s_merger.ports if not p.name.startswith("bit"))
    connect_points_routed(circuit, s_combined.abs_loc, s_pin.location(), proj.raw_project)
    
    # 6. Carry Logic
    # Cn pin to CLA_0.C0 and LCU.Cin
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, cn_pin, "io", clas[0], "C0", proj.raw_project)
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, cn_pin, "io", lcu, "Cin", proj.raw_project)
    
    # LCU.C1 -> CLA_1.C0
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "C1", clas[1], "C0", proj.raw_project)
    # LCU.C2 -> CLA_2.C0
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "C2", clas[2], "C0", proj.raw_project)
    # LCU.C3 -> CLA_3.C0
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "C3", clas[3], "C0", proj.raw_project)
    
    # 7. Final Outputs
    # LCU.C4 -> Cn+4 pin
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "C4", cn4_pin, "io", proj.raw_project)
    # LCU.P* -> Pf pin
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "P*", pf_pin, "io", proj.raw_project)
    # LCU.G* -> Gf pin
    connect_ports_routed(circuit, lcu, "G*", gf_pin, "io", proj.raw_project)

    # 8. Final touches
    editor.cleanup_detached_artifacts()
    proj.save(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_6_temp.circ")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade
from logisim_logic.rebuild_support import add_tunnel_to_port, add_wire, connect_points_routed

def main():
    proj = ProjectFacade.load(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_5_temp.circ")
    editor = proj.edit_circuit("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")
    circuit = editor.circuit
    
    # Components
    cla0 = editor.component("CLA_0")
    cla1 = editor.component("CLA_1")
    cla2 = editor.component("CLA_2")
    cla3 = editor.component("CLA_3")
    lcu = editor.component("LCU_0")
    
    x_pin = editor.component("X")
    y_pin = editor.component("Y")
    s_pin = editor.component("S")
    cn_pin = editor.component("Cn")
    cn4_pin = editor.component("Cn+4")
    pf_pin = editor.component("Pf")
    gf_pin = editor.component("Gf")
    
    x_split = editor.component("X_split")
    y_split = editor.component("Y_split")
    s_merg = editor.component("S_Merger")
    
    # 1. Connect Pins to Splitters
    # Direct wiring usually safe for pins and adjacent splitters
    add_wire(circuit, x_pin.location(), x_split.location())
    add_wire(circuit, y_pin.location(), y_split.location())
    
    # 2. Add Tunnels to Splitters (since legs are close and might overlap)
    # X bits
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, x_split, "bit0", "X0_3", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, x_split, "bit1", "X4_7", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, x_split, "bit2", "X8_11", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, x_split, "bit3", "X12_15", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    # Y bits
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, y_split, "bit0", "Y0_3", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, y_split, "bit1", "Y4_7", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, y_split, "bit2", "Y8_11", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, y_split, "bit3", "Y12_15", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    
    # 3. Add Tunnels to CLAs
    clas = [cla0, cla1, cla2, cla3]
    for i, cla in enumerate(clas):
        idx = f"{i*4}_{i*4+3}"
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "X", f"X{idx}", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "Y", f"Y{idx}", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "S", f"S{idx}", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "G*", f"g{i}", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "P*", f"p{i}", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
        # Carry-in
        if i == 0:
            add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "C0", "C_in", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
        else:
            add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cla, "C0", f"c{i}", 1, project=proj.raw_project)

    # 4. Add Tunnels to Merger
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, s_merg, "bit0", "S0_3", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, s_merg, "bit1", "S4_7", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, s_merg, "bit2", "S8_11", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, s_merg, "bit3", "S12_15", 4, project=proj.raw_project)
    # Merger combined output to S pin
    connect_points_routed(circuit, s_merg.location(), s_pin.location(), project=proj.raw_project)

    # 5. Add Tunnels to LCU
    # Port names for LCU based on inventory labels
    for i in range(4):
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, f"G{i+1}", f"g{i}", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
        add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, f"P{i+1}", f"p{i}", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "Cin", "C_in", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "C1", "c1", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "C2", "c2", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "C3", "c3", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "C4", "c_out", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "G*", "gf", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, lcu, "P*", "pf", 1, project=proj.raw_project)

    # 6. Final Pins
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cn_pin, "io", "C_in", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, cn4_pin, "io", "c_out", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, pf_pin, "io", "pf", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    add_tunnel_to_port(circuit, gf_pin, "io", "gf", 1, project=proj.raw_project)
    
    editor.cleanup_detached_artifacts()
    proj.save(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_9_temp.circ")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# 进位反馈回授
# LCU_0 的输出端口假设为 C1, C2, C3, C4, Gf, Pf。依据一般逻辑设计推断

connect("LCU_0.C3", "CLA_3.C0")

# 将 LCU_0 的 C4 作为最终进位

[Feedback] 验证失败: 经过结构和连通性验证，该16位快速加法器电路存在多处核心连接缺失，无法实现其逻辑功能：
1. 输入端挂空：输入引脚 X 和 Y（16位）虽然存在，但未与任何分线器或内部组件连接。

# 既然无法操作 XML，我们可以尝试手动将组件的 facing/loc 调整标准

[Feedback] 验证失败: 根据拓扑分析，电路 [16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）] 存在严重的结构和逻辑错误，无法通过验证：

1. **严重短路与位宽冲突**：网络 `net_1` 将 16 位输出引脚 `S`、1 位输入引脚 `Cn`、1 位输出引脚 `Cn+4` 以及一个 16 位分线器的组合端全部连接在一起，这在逻辑上是错误的，且在 Logisim 中会由于位宽不匹配导致红色连线（冲突）。
2. **组件端口连接混乱**：网络 `net_0` 错误地将多个 4 位快速加法器（CLA）的 `S`、`G*`、`P*` 端口以及分线器的多个分支端口短接。在正确的加法电路中，这些信号应是相互独立的。
3. **LCU 子电路接口失效**：实例 `LCU_0`（4位先行进位电路）在主电路中仅呈现为一个名为 `io` 的单一端口，且未建立任何有效逻辑连接。该子电路本应负责接收各组的 $P$、$G$ 信号并生成各组进位，但目前它处于悬空状态。
4. **总线处理错误**：输入引脚 `X` 和 `Y` 虽然连接到了分线器表面上，但从拓扑看，其分支并未正确引导至对应的 CLA 单元输入端。

修复建议：
- 重新检查各组件的端口映射，确保 $G_i$ 和 $P_i$ 信号正确连接至 LCU。
- 在 LCU 生成 $C_1, C_2, C_3$ 后，将其回馈至对应 CLA 的 $C_0$ 端口。
- 使用正确的 Splitter/Merger 逻辑合并 4 位和 16 位信号，严禁将不同性质或位宽的端口直接相连。

# 获取编辑器实例
editor = ProjectFacade.get_editor("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")

# 1. 删除所有 Splitter 组件
splitters = [c for c in editor.get_all_components() if c.name == "Splitter"]
for s in splitters:
    editor.delete_component(s)

# 在 Logisim 中，单纯删除组件会删除连接的线体，
# 但为了彻底确保没有残留的导线(wires)，我们根据 API 描述清理网络。
# 注意：editor.clear_wires() 是常规操作，若无此方法，遍历 components 集合并只保留需要的

# 方案：直接连接引脚(Pin)和子电路组件引脚。
# 注意：子电路引脚名通常是 Pin 所在位置的 label

# 1. 连接 Cn 到 LCU_0 的 Cin 端 (外部直接通过 Pin 连接)
# 查找 LCU_0 的输入 Pin，直接接在一起
# 根据 step_3_temp 的结构，我们需要识别 LCU_0 内部的端口映射
# 由于直接使用组件名.Port名失败，我们尝试使用坐标或隧道

# 修复：确认 ports，针对 LCU_0 进行连接
# 子电路内部的引脚可以通过其所在的绝对坐标或特定的端口名称映射：
# 目前看起来该先行进位电路没有暴露正确的端口给 main 电路。
# 既然 LCU_0 内部使用了隧道(Tunnel)，我们直接连接外部信号到对应的隧道。

# 重新考虑：Step_3 的连接可能需要通过 Tunnel 实现，如果直接用 .Port 报错。
# 但脚本接口只支持 connect("Comp.Port", ...) 或坐标。

from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade, RawAttribute
from logisim_logic.model import XmlFragment

def fix_lcu_appearance(circuit):
    # Map of label to Pin location
    pin_map = {}
    for comp in circuit.components:
        if comp.name == "Pin":
            label = comp.get("label")
            if label:
                pin_map[label] = comp.loc
    
    print(f"Pins found: {list(pin_map.keys())}")
    
    # Standard appearance: a rectangle with pins on left/right/top/bottom
    # Left: Inputs (G1, P1, G2, P2, G3, P3, G4, P4)
    # Right: Outputs (C1, C2, C3, C4, G*, P*)
    # Bottom: Cin
    
    # We'll create a simple appearance XML
    shapes = []
    # Rectangle
    shapes.append(XmlFragment.from_element_dict({
        "tag": "rect",
        "fill": "none",
        "height": "160",
        "stroke": "#000000",
        "stroke-width": "2",
        "width": "120",
        "x": "50",
        "y": "50"
    }))
    
    # Port assignments
    port_layout = {
        "P1": (50, 60), "G1": (50, 70),
        "P2": (50, 90), "G2": (50, 100),
        "P3": (50, 120), "G3": (50, 130),
        "P4": (50, 150), "G4": (50, 160),
        "Cin": (110, 210),
        "C1": (170, 70), "C2": (170, 90), "C3": (170, 110), "C4": (170, 130),
        "G*": (170, 160), "P*": (170, 180)
    }
    
    for label, appearance_loc in port_layout.items():
        if label in pin_map:
            pin_loc = pin_map[label]
            shapes.append(XmlFragment.from_element_dict({
                "tag": "circ-port",
                "height": "8",
                "pin-location": f"{pin_loc[0]},{pin_loc[1]}",
                "width": "8",
                "x": str(appearance_loc[0] - 4),
                "y": str(appearance_loc[1] - 4)
            }))
    
    circuit.appearance.shapes = shapes
    print("LCU Appearance updated.")

facade = ProjectFacade.load(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_6_temp.circ")
lcu = facade.project.circuit("4位先行进位电路")
fix_lcu_appearance(lcu)
facade.save(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_7_temp.circ")

import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade, RawAttribute
from logisim_logic.model import XmlFragment, RawCircuit
from logisim_logic.logic_builder import LogicCircuitBuilder
from logisim_logic.rebuild_support import ordered_splitter_attrs

def fix_lcu_appearance(circuit):
    pin_map = {}
    for comp in circuit.components:
        if comp.name == "Pin":
            label = comp.get("label")
            if label:
                pin_map[label] = comp.loc
    
    shapes = []
    # Rect
    rect = ET.Element("rect", {
        "fill": "none", "height": "160", "stroke": "#000000", "stroke-width": "2",
        "width": "120", "x": "50", "y": "50"
    })
    shapes.append(XmlFragment.from_element(rect))
    
    # Port assignments: Input Left, Output Right
    port_layout = {
        "P1": (50, 60), "G1": (50, 70),
        "P2": (50, 90), "G2": (50, 100),
        "P3": (50, 120), "G3": (50, 130),
        "P4": (50, 150), "G4": (50, 160),
        "Cin": (110, 210),
        "C1": (170, 70), "C2": (170, 90), "C3": (170, 110), "C4": (170, 130),
        "G*": (170, 160), "P*": (170, 180)
    }
    
    for label, appearance_loc in port_layout.items():
        if label in pin_map:
            pin_loc = pin_map[label]
            port = ET.Element("circ-port", {
                "height": "8", "width": "8",
                "pin-location": f"{pin_loc[0]},{pin_loc[1]}",
                "x": str(appearance_loc[0] - 4),
                "y": str(appearance_loc[1] - 4)
            })
            shapes.append(XmlFragment.from_element(port))
    
    circuit.appearance.shapes = shapes

def run():
    facade = ProjectFacade.load(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_6_temp.circ")
    project = facade.project
    
    # Fix LCU appearance first
    lcu_ckt = project.circuit("4位先行进位电路")
    fix_lcu_appearance(lcu_ckt)
    
    # Main circuit name
    target_name = "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）"
    
    # Create Builder
    # Use allow_tunnel_fallback=True if layout is too dense, but here we'll try to let it route
    builder = LogicCircuitBuilder(target_name, project=project)
    
    # Inputs
    builder.add_instance("X", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "X", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 50))
    builder.add_instance("Y", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "Y", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 150))
    builder.add_instance("Cn", "Pin", {"label": "Cn", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 250))
    
    # Splitters for X, Y
    # Group 0: 0-3, Group 1: 4-7, Group 2: 8-11, Group 3: 12-15
    builder.add_instance("X_split", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4]), loc=(150, 50))
    builder.add_instance("Y_split", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4]), loc=(150, 150))
    
    builder.connect("X.io", "X_split.combined")
    builder.connect("Y.io", "Y_split.combined")
    
    # 4 CLAs
    for i in range(4):
        builder.add_instance(f"CLA_{i}", "4位快速加法器（1）", {"label": f"CLA_{i}"}, loc=(350, 50 + i * 120))
        builder.connect(f"X_split.split{i}", f"CLA_{i}.X")
        builder.connect(f"Y_split.split{i}", f"CLA_{i}.Y")
    
    # LCU
    builder.add_instance("LCU", "4位先行进位电路", {"label": "LCU"}, loc=(600, 250))
    
    # Connections between CLAs and LCU
    # CLA_0 (low) -> LCU G1, P1
    # CLA_1 -> LCU G2, P2 ...
    for i in range(4):
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.G*", f"LCU.G{i+1}")
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.P*", f"LCU.P{i+1}")
    
    builder.connect("Cn.io", "LCU.Cin")
    builder.connect("Cn.io", "CLA_0.C0")
    
    # Carry path
    builder.connect("LCU.C1", "CLA_1.C0")
    builder.connect("LCU.C2", "CLA_2.C0")
    builder.connect("LCU.C3", "CLA_3.C0")
    
    # Final Outputs
    builder.add_instance("S", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "S", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(800, 50))
    builder.add_instance("S_merger", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4], facing="west"), loc=(700, 50))
    builder.connect("S_merger.combined", "S.io")
    
    for i in range(4):
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.S", f"S_merger.split{i}")
        
    builder.add_instance("Cn4", "Pin", {"label": "Cn+4", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(800, 250))
    builder.connect("LCU.C4", "Cn4.io")
    
    builder.add_instance("Pf", "Pin", {"label": "Pf", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(800, 300))
    builder.connect("LCU.P*", "Pf.io")
    
    builder.add_instance("Gf", "Pin", {"label": "Gf", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(800, 350))
    builder.connect("LCU.G*", "Gf.io")

    # Rebuild circuit
    new_circuit = builder.build()
    
    # Preserve appearance from old circuit if possible
    # We'll just replace the original circuit in project
    project.replace_circuit(new_circuit)
    
    facade.save(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_8_temp.circ")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run()

def run():
    # Load from the previously "successful" but seemingly unchanged file
    facade = ProjectFacade.load(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_8_temp.circ")
    project = facade.project
    
    # Check LCU
    lcu_ckt = project.circuit("4位先行进位电路")
    fix_lcu_appearance(lcu_ckt)
    
    target_name = "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）"
    
    # Manual cleanup of the target circuit
    target_ckt = project.circuit(target_name)
    target_ckt.components = []
    target_ckt.wires = []
    
    builder = LogicCircuitBuilder(target_name, project=project)
    
    # Define locations
    # X, Y, Cn on the left
    builder.add_instance("X", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "X", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 50))
    builder.add_instance("Y", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "Y", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 200))
    builder.add_instance("Cn", "Pin", {"label": "Cn", "facing": "east"}, loc=(50, 350))
    
    # Splitters
    builder.add_instance("X_split", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4], facing="east"), loc=(150, 50))
    builder.add_instance("Y_split", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4], facing="east"), loc=(150, 200))
    
    builder.connect("X.io", "X_split.combined")
    builder.connect("Y.io", "Y_split.combined")
    
    # CLAs
    for i in range(4):
        # Spacing them out for routing
        builder.add_instance(f"CLA_{i}", "4位快速加法器（1）", {"label": f"CLA_{i}"}, loc=(400, 50 + i * 150))
        builder.connect(f"X_split.split{i}", f"CLA_{i}.X")
        builder.connect(f"Y_split.split{i}", f"CLA_{i}.Y")
    
    # LCU
    builder.add_instance("LCU", "4位先行进位电路", {"label": "LCU"}, loc=(700, 400))
    
    # Connect
    builder.connect("Cn.io", "LCU.Cin")
    builder.connect("Cn.io", "CLA_0.C0")
    
    for i in range(4):
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.G*", f"LCU.G{i+1}")
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.P*", f"LCU.P{i+1}")
    
    builder.connect("LCU.C1", "CLA_1.C0")
    builder.connect("LCU.C2", "CLA_2.C0")
    builder.connect("LCU.C3", "CLA_3.C0")
    
    # Outputs
    builder.add_instance("S", "Pin", {"width": "16", "label": "S", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(1000, 50))
    builder.add_instance("S_merger", "Splitter", ordered_splitter_attrs(16, [4, 4, 4, 4], facing="west"), loc=(900, 50))
    builder.connect("S_merger.combined", "S.io")
    
    for i in range(4):
        builder.connect(f"CLA_{i}.S", f"S_merger.split{i}")
        
    builder.add_instance("Cn4", "Pin", {"label": "Cn+4", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(1000, 350))
    builder.connect("LCU.C4", "Cn4.io")
    
    builder.add_instance("Pf", "Pin", {"label": "Pf", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(1000, 400))
    builder.connect("LCU.P*", "Pf.io")
    
    builder.add_instance("Gf", "Pin", {"label": "Gf", "output": "true", "facing": "west"}, loc=(1000, 450))
    builder.connect("LCU.G*", "Gf.io")

    built_ckt = builder.build()
    
    # Transfer components and wires from built_ckt back to the project's circuit
    target_ckt.components = built_ckt.components
    target_ckt.wires = built_ckt.wires
    
    facade.save(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_9_temp.circ")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run()

# 修复 '4位先行进位电路' 的 Appearance 设置
# 这是一个 XML 结构修改任务，我们通过注入脚本来修改 circ-port 映射

def fix_appearance():
    # 获取组件实例映射
    # 所有的 Pin 都有对应的 ID
    # 按照指示，我们需要确保以下 15 个引脚映射到外观
    # 端口包括: G1, G2, G3, G4, P1, P2, P3, P4, Cin 及 C1, C2, C3, C4, G*, P*
    
    # 在 Logisim XML 中，外观在 <appear > 标签下，内部是 <circ-port>
    # 我们调用 editor 的相关方法来确保它们存在
    
    # 根据已获取的组件 ID:
    # G1: 4
    # G2: 33
    # G3: 8
    # G4: 45
    # P1: 55
    # P2: 9
    # P3: 34
    # P4: 39
    # Cin: 36
    # C1: 54
    # C2: 56
    # C3: 3
    # C4: 52
    # G*: 6
    # P*: 63
    
    pin_ids = [4, 33, 8, 45, 55, 9, 34, 39, 36, 54, 56, 3, 52, 6, 63]
    
    for pid in pin_ids:
        # 修改引脚的外观属性或确保其被包含
        # 在 LogisimAPI 中，我们通常不需要手动操作 XML
        # 但如果外观映射丢失，我们可以重新设置其标签或强制刷新
        pass

    # 核心逻辑：确保这些引脚都在外观中
    # 实际上由于这些已经是电路内的原始 Pin，只需保存即可保持其外观映射
    # 若被损坏，调用 editor 对外观进行同步更新
    # 鉴于 API 限制，我们将通过重命名或设置属性来强制更新
    
    # 这一步主要是告诉用户，我们已识别出这些引脚
    print("Found pins to map: G1..G4, P1..P4, Cin, C1..C4, G*, P*")

add_instance("Pin", (1200, 250), attrs={"facing": "west", "label": "G_out", "width": "1"})
add_instance("Pin", (1200, 300), attrs={"facing": "west", "label": "P_out", "width": "1"})

# 2. 放置分线器 (Splitter)

add_instance("Splitter", (150, 200), attrs={"facing": "east", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitWidth": "4", "label": "splitY"})

# 3. 放置 4 个 CLA 实例 (假设子电路名为 "CLA") 和 1 个 LCU 实例 ("LCU")
for i in range(4):
    add_instance("CLA", (400, 50 + i * 100), attrs={"label": f"CLA_{i}"})
add_instance("LCU", (700, 200), attrs={"label": "LCU"})

# 4. 连接逻辑
connect("X", "splitX")
connect("Y", "splitY")

# 连接 CLA_i 的 X/Y 到对应分线器端口
for i in range(4):
    connect(f"splitX.{i}", f"CLA_{i}.X")
    connect(f"splitY.{i}", f"CLA_{i}.Y")
    # 连接 CLA_i 的 G/P 到 LCU 的 Gi/Pi (假设端口为 G, P)
    connect(f"CLA_{i}.G", f"LCU.G{i+1}")
    connect(f"CLA_{i}.P", f"LCU.P{i+1}")
    # CLA 求和输出连接
    connect(f"CLA_{i}.S", f"S[{i*4}:{(i+1)*4}]") # 简化表示，实际应通过分线器汇聚输出

# 连接控制位
connect("Cn", "LCU.Cin")
connect("Cn", "CLA_0.C0")
connect("LCU.C1", "CLA_1.C0")
connect("LCU.C2", "CLA_2.C0")
connect("LCU.C3", "CLA_3.C0")

# 汇聚 LCU 输出
connect("LCU.C4", "C4")
connect("LCU.G", "G_out")
connect("LCU.P", "P_out")

from logisim_logic import *

# 1. 定义布局归一化工具类
def normalize_padding(circuit_name):
    editor = CircuitEditor(circuit_name)
    components = editor.get_all_components()
    # 简单的坐标网格化对齐: 将坐标对齐至 10 的倍数
    for comp in components:
        x, y = comp.loc
        new_x = (x // 10) * 10
        new_y = (y // 10) * 10
        if (x, y) != (new_x, new_y):
            editor.move_component(comp, (new_x, new_y))
    return editor

# 2. 检查位宽冲突 (16位与1位连接检查)
def find_width_conflicts(editor):
    conflicts = []
    # 获取逻辑拓扑
    nets = editor.get_topology()
    for net in nets:
        # 获取连接到该网络的端口及其位宽
        ports = net.ports
        widths = set(p.width for p in ports)
        if len(widths) > 1 and (16 in widths and 1 in widths):
            conflicts.append(f"Network {net.id} has mixed widths: {widths}")
    return conflicts

# 3. 执行任务
editor = normalize_padding("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间串行）（1）")
conflicts = find_width_conflicts(editor)
if conflicts:
    print(f"检测到位宽冲突: {conflicts}")
else:
    print("未发现位宽冲突。")

# 4. 持久化保存
editor.save_circuit()

# 简化方案：加载工程并操作
from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade, CircuitEditor

project = ProjectFacade("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_3_temp.circ")
# 使用快捷方法访问电路对象
circuit = project.get_circuit_by_name("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间串行）（1）")
editor = CircuitEditor(project, circuit)

# 坐标对齐 (简单的对齐逻辑)
components = editor.get_all_components()
for comp in components:
    # 假设获取到组件，修正位置 (10单位对齐)
    loc = comp.get_location()
    new_loc = ((loc[0] // 10) * 10, (loc[1] // 10) * 10)
    if loc != new_loc:
        editor.update_component_location(comp, new_loc)

# 保存
editor.save()

from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade, CircuitEditor

project = ProjectFacade("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_3_temp.circ")

# 获取并操作
circuit = project.get_circuit("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间串行）（1）")
editor = CircuitEditor(project, circuit)

# 执行归一化
components = editor.get_all_components()
for comp in components:
    # 假设组件对象支持 get_location/set_location
    loc = comp.get_location()
    new_loc = ((loc[0] // 10) * 10, (loc[1] // 10) * 10)
    if loc != new_loc:
        comp.set_location(new_loc)

editor.save()

# 1. 放置分线器
add_instance("Splitter", (120, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "label": "X_split"})
add_instance("Splitter", (180, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "label": "Y_split"})

# 2. 连接 Pin 输入到分线器
connect("X", "X_split")
connect("Y", "Y_split")

# 3. 连接分线器输出到各 CLA 组件
# 任务要求: X[0:3] -> CLA_3.X, X[4:7] -> CLA_2.X, X[8:11] -> CLA_1.X, X[12:15] -> CLA_0.X (假设X是从高位到低位或者反之，按逻辑顺序连接)
# 修正：通常Logisim Splitter的第0个引脚是最低位，按照指令进行连接
connect("X_split.0", "CLA_3.X")
connect("X_split.1", "CLA_2.X")
connect("X_split.2", "CLA_1.X")
connect("X_split.3", "CLA_0.X")

connect("Y_split.0", "CLA_3.Y")
connect("Y_split.1", "CLA_2.Y")
connect("Y_split.2", "CLA_1.Y")
connect("Y_split.3", "CLA_0.Y")

# 放置分线器

add_instance("Splitter", (180, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "label": "Y_split"})

# 直接连接到组件的实例名(label)
# 注意：connect 接收的字符串格式为 "Label.PortName" 或 (x,y)
# 由于 Pin 组件可能没有端口名，直接使用标签连接可能失效，改为连接到 (x, y) 坐标
# 但上面用坐标连接失败是因为不能传入元组，需检查用法。根据手册：支持 "InstLabel.PortName" 或 (x, y)
# 修正 connect 调用：connect((70, 80), (120, 150)) -- 改为连接两个组件实例的 Label
# 上一个错误是因为 `connect` 内部处理坐标时把坐标解析为了组件对象，导致 AttributeError。
# 尝试使用 Label
connect("X", "X_split")
connect("Y", "Y_split")

# 连接分线器到 CLA 组件(已知的 label)
connect("X_split", "CLA_3")
connect("X_split", "CLA_2")
connect("X_split", "CLA_1")
connect("X_split", "CLA_0")

connect("Y_split", "CLA_3")
connect("Y_split", "CLA_2")
connect("Y_split", "CLA_1")
connect("Y_split", "CLA_0")

# 在 (120, 150) 添加 X 分线器 (16位进, 4x4位出)
# 在 (180, 150) 添加 Y 分线器 (16位进, 4x4位出)
# Logisim 中组件的输入引脚通常没有具体名字，或者直接用组件名代替，此处尝试直接用 "Splitter"
# 但我们需要确保端口连接正确
add_instance("Splitter", (120, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "label": "X_split"})
add_instance("Splitter", (180, 150), attrs={"facing": "south", "fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "label": "Y_split"})

# Logisim 分线器输出端口通常名为 "0", "1", "2", "3" 等
# 将 X[0:3], X[4:7], X[8:11], X[12:15] 连接到 CLA
# 这里的 "0", "1" 指的是 Splitter 的端口索引
connect("X_split.0", "CLA_3.X")
connect("X_split.1", "CLA_2.X")
connect("X_split.2", "CLA_1.X")
connect("X_split.3", "CLA_0.X")

connect("Y_split.0", "CLA_3.Y")
connect("Y_split.1", "CLA_2.Y")
connect("Y_split.2", "CLA_1.Y")
connect("Y_split.3", "CLA_0.Y")

from logisim_logic import CircuitEditor, ProjectFacade

def inspect_circuit():
    project = ProjectFacade("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_4_temp.circ")
    circuit = project.get_circuit("16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")
    
    print("Components in 16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）:")
    for comp in circuit.get_components():

    # Also check the wires
    print("\nWires:")
    for wire in circuit.get_wires():
        print(f"Wire: {wire.p1} to {wire.p2}")

from logisim_logic import ProjectFacade

def inspect():
    # Note: ProjectFacade might not be used this way, let's try a different approach if it fails.
    # Actually, the tool environment usually pre-loads things.
    # Let's try to list circuits.
    import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
    tree = ET.parse(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_4_temp.circ")
    root = tree.getroot()
    
    for circuit in root.findall('circuit'):
        if circuit.get('name') == "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）":
            print(f"Circuit: {circuit.get('name')}")
            for comp in circuit.findall('comp'):
                print(f"Comp: {comp.get('name')}, Label: {comp.find('a[@name=\"label\"]')}")
                if comp.find('a[@name="label"]') is not None:
                    print(f"  Label: {comp.find('a[@name=\"label\"]').get('val')}")
            for wire in circuit.findall('wire'):
                print(f"Wire: {wire.get('from')} to {wire.get('to')}")

盘点完成。以下是所涉及电路的关键引脚和位宽信息：

### 16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）
*   **输入:**
    *   `X`: 16位
    *   `Y`: 16位
    *   `Cn`: 1位
*   **输出:**
    *   `S`: 16位
    *   `Cn+4`: 1位
    *   `Pf`: 1位
    *   `Gf`: 1位

### 4位快速加法器（1）
*   **输入:**
    *   `X`: 4位
    *   `Y`: 4位
    *   `C0`: 1位
*   **输出:**
    *   `S`: 4位
    *   `C4`: 1位
    *   `C3`: 1位
    *   `OF`: 1位
    *   `G*`: 1位
    *   `P*`: 1位

### 4位先行进位电路 (LCU)
*   **输入:**
    *   `G4`, `P4`, `G3`, `P3`, `G2`, `P2`, `G1`, `P1`, `Cin`: 每个均为1位
    *   *注: 实际逻辑中，LCU通常接收各组的生成(G)和传递(P)信号及初始进位，输出各级进位(C4, C3, C2, C1)及成组信号(G*, P*)*
*   **输出:**
    *   `C4`, `C3`, `C2`, `C1`: 各1位
    *   `G*`, `P*`: 各1位

import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

def count_wires(file_path, circuit_name):
    tree = ET.parse(file_path)
    root = tree.getroot()
    for circuit in root.findall('circuit'):
        if circuit.get('name') == circuit_name:
            wires = circuit.findall('wire')
            print(f"DEBUG: Found {len(wires)} wires in circuit {circuit_name}")
            return len(wires)
    return 0

count_wires("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_3_temp.circ", "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")

from logisim_logic import load_project

project = load_project("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_3_temp.circ")

def check_circuit(name):
    ckt = project.circuit(name)
    print(f"Circuit: {name}")
    print(f"  Appearance items: {len(ckt.appearances)}")
    # In raw project, circuit.appearances is usually a list of XmlFragment or similar
    if hasattr(ckt, 'appearance'):
        print(f"  Appearance: {ckt.appearance}")
    
    # Check pins
    pins = [c for c in ckt.components if c.name == "Pin"]
    for p in pins:
        print(f"  Pin label: {p.get('label')}, loc: {p.loc}, width: {p.get('width')}, output: {p.get('output')}")

check_circuit("4位快速加法器（1）")
check_circuit("4位先行进位电路")

# 配置分线器：incoming=16位，4路输出
# 分线规则：bit[0..3] -> 输出端3, ..., bit[12..15] -> 输出端0

    "facing": "north",
    "fanout": "4",
    "incoming": "16",
    "bit1": "1000",                # 这一步依赖具体库的参数名，通常可以直接用 bit0-3 映射属性
    "label": "X_Splitter"
})

    "facing": "north",
    "fanout": "4",
    "incoming": "16",
    "bit1": "1000",
    "label": "Y_Splitter"
})

# 电路构建：并行进位链逻辑
# 检查当前的逻辑连接需求：
# 1. 全局进位：Cn (50, 110) 已映射为 Cn 引脚
# 2. 需求指示：Cn引脚(480, 80) -> 实际上在本电路中，Cn引脚位于(50, 110)
# 修正：根据 inventory，Cn引脚位于 (50, 110)，目标为 LCU.Cin 和 Block0.C0 (LSB加法器)

# 执行连接
# 注意：在 Logisim 中，端口名称需要根据子电路实际定义来访问。
# 若内部端口访问有问题，使用坐标连接。

# 1. 全局进位：Cn 连至 LCU.Cin 和 Block0.C0
connect("Cn", "LCU.Cin")
connect("Cn", "Block0.C0")

# 2. 组间进位：LCU.C1 -> Block1.C0, LCU.C2 -> Block2.C0, LCU.C3 -> Block3.C0
connect("LCU.C1", "Block1.C0")
connect("LCU.C2", "Block2.C0")
connect("LCU.C3", "Block3.C0")

# 3. 进位生成与传递：CLA->LCU 映射
# CLA_3 -> Block0, CLA_2 -> Block1, CLA_1 -> Block2, CLA_0 -> Block3
connect("Block0.G", "LCU.G1")
connect("Block0.P", "LCU.P1")
connect("Block1.G", "LCU.G2")
connect("Block1.P", "LCU.P2")
connect("Block2.G", "LCU.G3")
connect("Block2.P", "LCU.P3")
connect("Block3.G", "LCU.G4")
connect("Block3.P", "LCU.P4")

# 4. 最终输出
connect("LCU.C4", "Cn+4")
connect("LCU.P", "Pf")
connect("LCU.G", "Gf")

import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET

tree = ET.parse(r"D:\Scripts\autozhy_logisim_report\tests\cases\design\step_7_temp.circ")
root = tree.getroot()

# Find the main circuit
circuit_name = "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）"
circuit = None
for circ in root.findall("circuit"):
    if circ.get("name") == circuit_name:
        circuit = circ
        break

if circuit is not None:
    # Check for width conflicts in wires (basic heuristic: Logisim doesn't store width in wires, 
    # but we can check if splitters/pins match)
    pins = []
    for comp in circuit.findall("comp"):
        name = comp.get("name")
        label = ""
        width = "1"
        for attr in comp.findall("a"):
            if attr.get("name") == "label":
                label = attr.get("val")
            if attr.get("name") == "width":
                width = attr.get("val")
        if name == "Pin":
            pins.append((label, width))
            print(f"Pin {label}: width {width}")
    
    # Check subcircuits
    for comp in circuit.findall("comp"):
        name = comp.get("name")
        if "加法器" in name or "进位" in name:
            print(f"Subcircuit instance: {name}")

    # Check wires for obvious issues (disconnected)
    wires = circuit.findall("wire")
    print(f"Total wires: {len(wires)}")
else:
    print("Circuit not found")

# 清理 main 电路（假设通过重建逻辑覆盖主要组件）
# 1. 实例化核心组件
# 4个 4位快速加法器
for i in range(4):
    add_instance("4位快速加法器（1）", (300, 100 + i * 100), attrs={"label": f"Block{i}"})

# 1个 4位先行进位电路
add_instance("4位先行进位电路", (600, 250), attrs={"label": "LCU"})

# 2. 实例化输入/输出引脚
add_instance("Pin", (50, 100), attrs={"label": "X", "width": "16"})
add_instance("Pin", (50, 150), attrs={"label": "Y", "width": "16"})
add_instance("Pin", (50, 200), attrs={"label": "Cn", "width": "1"})
add_instance("Pin", (800, 100), attrs={"label": "S", "width": "16", "facing": "west"})
add_instance("Pin", (800, 150), attrs={"label": "Cn+4", "width": "1", "facing": "west"})
add_instance("Pin", (800, 200), attrs={"label": "Pf", "width": "1", "facing": "west"})
add_instance("Pin", (800, 250), attrs={"label": "Gf", "width": "1", "facing": "west"})

# 3. 实例化分线器和汇聚器
add_instance("Splitter", (150, 100), attrs={"fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitwidth": "4", "label": "X_Split"})
add_instance("Splitter", (150, 150), attrs={"fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitwidth": "4", "label": "Y_Split"})
add_instance("Splitter", (700, 100), attrs={"fanout": "4", "incoming": "16", "bitwidth": "4", "facing": "west", "label": "S_Merge"})

# 4. 连接逻辑
connect("X", "X_Split")
connect("Y", "Y_Split")

for i in range(4):
    connect(f"X_Split.{i}", f"Block{i}.X")
    connect(f"Y_Split.{i}", f"Block{i}.Y")
    connect(f"Block{i}.Gi", f"LCU.G{i+1}")
    connect(f"Block{i}.Pi", f"LCU.P{i+1}")
    connect(f"Block{i}.S", f"S_Merge.{i}")

connect("Cn", "LCU.Cin")
connect("Cn", "Block0.C0")
connect("LCU.C1", "Block1.C0")

    connect(f"X_Split.{i}", f"Block{i}.X")
    connect(f"Y_Split.{i}", f"Block{i}.Y")
    connect(f"Block{i}.Gi", f"LCU.G{i+1}")
    connect(f"Block{i}.Pi", f"LCU.P{i+1}")

connect("LCU.Pf", "Pf")

[Feedback] 验证失败: 根据结构和逻辑分析，16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）电路验证未通过。以下是详细的修复清单：

1. **逻辑连接完全缺失**：电路中虽然放置了输入输出引脚和四个 4 位快速加法器（CLA）组件，但没有任何导线（Nets）连接，所有端口均处于悬空状态。
2. **缺少关键进位组件**：要实现“组间并行”进位，必须包含一个 `4位先行进位电路` (LCU/74182) 来接收各组的 P/G 信号并生成组间进位信号。当前电路中缺失此核心组件。
3. **缺少位宽转换逻辑**：16 位的 X、Y 输入引脚和 S 输出引脚未通过分线器 (Splitter) 进行位拆分与合并，无法正确连接到 4 位的子加法器端口。
4. **端口定义与需求不符**：参考设计要求输出 S、C16、C15、OF、G*、P*，而当前电路引脚为 Cn+4、Pf、Gf，且缺乏计算溢出 (OF) 和最高位进位 (C15, C16) 的逻辑电路（如 XOR 门）。
5. **结构不完整**：电路目前仅是一个组件堆放的模板，未完成从串行进位（组内并行）到完全并行进位（组间并行）的逻辑升级。

    "Pf": {"loc": (560, 120), "width": 1, "output": True},
    "Gf": {"loc": (560, 160), "width": 1, "output": True}
}

# 2. 删除并重新添加
for old_label, info in pins_map.items():
    comp = find_component(old_label)
    if comp:
        delete_component(comp)
        
        # 映射新 Label
        new_labels = {"Cn": "C0", "Cn+4": "C16", "Pf": "P*", "Gf": "G*"}
        
        add_instance("Pin", info["loc"], attrs={
            "label": new_labels[old_label],
            "width": str(info["width"]),
            "output": str(info["output"]).lower()
        })

# 3. 添加新引脚
add_instance("Pin", (600, 200), attrs={"label": "C15", "output": "true", "width": "1"})
add_instance("Pin", (600, 240), attrs={"label": "OF", "output": "true", "width": "1"})

save_circuit()

from logisim_logic.circuit import CircuitEditor
import json

def check_wires(project_path, circuit_name):
    editor = CircuitEditor(project_path)
    circuit = editor.get_circuit(circuit_name)
    wires = circuit.get_wires()
    print(f"Wire count: {len(wires)}")
    for wire in wires:
        print(f"Wire: {wire}")

check_wires("D:\\Scripts\\autozhy_logisim_report\\tests\\cases\\design\\step_4_temp.circ", "16位快速加法器（组内并行、组间并行）")
